Process for adding new types
1. create a new addQuestion<type> function for that type
2. Update API with any new getters for additional type fields
3. update the addNewQuestion switch statement in the API
4. create an answer validation function for the submitAnswer API call
5. update the submitAnswer switch statement to use the validation function  ^XKbILJk9

Power Sync Worker ^zfH6d3Oz

The Power Sync Worker, will be the entry point for the background process responsible for syncing information with the cloud. Generally, all local data will sync with the cloud. 
1. Any User can contribute content, but this content get's synced with an intermediary SQL table. This question_answer pair table will be subject to manual review. . .

2. Question from this intermediary table will be manually reviewed, if they fail review, they will be marked as such and stay in the table.

3. If the question answer pair passes review it will move to the central pair table that will actually sync back to all user's (this allows user's to add their own content locally, working around user authorization for contributors)
 ^67xOx5cL

answer element ^wtV9wdax

answer element ^wsUDigmQ

answer element ^zHTcH5zh

1. double-click on question or answer element allows
edit of that entry
2. double-click of option text allows edit
3. if element is an image, user is prompted to select a new 
image
4. elements are re-orderable, use the same drag and drop 
implementation as the sort_order widget
5. Entering text using a textfield, when the user presses enter
the element/option is submitted to the bottom of the element list,
focus should remain on these fields after pressing enter so the 
user can immediately enter a new option
6. the option elements should have a toggle button on the left.
depending on the question type, this either toggles it as the correct option,
submits it as the only correct option, 
or is not displayed (like with sort_order example)
